	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#9d7f69>巴</color>", NULL, "<color=#9d7f69>Tomoe</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s14/28/vt4bb_tomoe2518", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「はぁっ、はぁっ、はぁっ……！！」",
			NULL, "\"Haah, haah, haah...!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r塚田の身体を抱えて、巴は海面から波止場の一角へとにじり寄り、…運良く発見した梯子を伝って陸に上がる。そして、
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "塚田の身体を抱えて、巴は海面から波止場の一角へとにじり寄り、…運良く発見した梯子を伝って陸に上がる。そして、",
			NULL, "While holding Tsukada's body, Tomoe swam across the surface of the sea to a corner of the wharf... where thankfully, she spotted a ladder that led up to the surface. And then,", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	PlaySE(3, "down2", 256, 64);
	ShakeScreen( 1, 15, 15, 2, 0, );
	Wait( 150 );

//巴rvS14/28/VT4Bb_tomoe2519.「塚田さん…！kvS14/28/VT4Bb_tomoe2520.　しっかりしてください、塚田さん……っ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#9d7f69>巴</color>", NULL, "<color=#9d7f69>Tomoe</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s14/28/vt4bb_tomoe2519", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「塚田さん…！",
			NULL, "\"Tsukada-san...!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s14/28/vt4bb_tomoe2520", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　しっかりしてください、塚田さん……っ！！」",
			NULL, " Hang in there, Tsukada-san...!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//rその叫び、…というにはか細い声を振り絞って、喉からほとばしらせた直後。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "その叫び、…というにはか細い声を振り絞って、喉からほとばしらせた直後。",
			NULL, "After that shout... Tomoe's voice became very thin, and she coughed up the water inside her throat.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r巴は完全に…意識を、失った。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "巴は完全に…意識を、失った。",
			NULL, "Then, Tomoe collapsed... and completely lost consciousness.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
